name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Business travelers
info:34 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 15, 2024
msg:Having been to Nanjing many times, I feel a little sad that I came to Nanjing Grand Hotel so late. The English name of the hotel is NANJING GRAND HOTEL. The translation of GRAND into Grand Hotel corresponds to the history of Nanjing itself, which is really perfect. The main building of the hotel faces north and south. I stayed on the south side this time, and the Wutaishan Stadium was outside the window. You can see the tasteful stands and running tracks. The famous Pioneer Bookstore is a sunken building, which is under the stadium, just south of the hotel. Whether it is sports or reading, it is very convenient. The back of the hotel is the Nandonggua City and Beidonggua City communities, where there is also a very beautiful place, Nanjing No. 2 Kindergarten. If you live at the north gate of the hotel, it should be very happy to see the children going to kindergarten in the morning. The doorman of the hotel feels great, and all the employees are very polite. The building is very tasteful, with many Japanese styles. The guest rooms are not big or new, but comfortable and just right. The breakfast is also great, with beef noodles, chicken soup noodles, duck blood vermicelli, green willow house vegetarian buns, and not too sweet eight-treasure porridge. Next time I come to Nanjing, I will probably choose here again.

The room card set was left in October last year, and it has not been discovered by the cleaning staff for half a year! ! ! The next day, I reported this problem to the front desk. After communicating with the lobby manager, I changed to an executive room (Figure 1). Although the area is not as large as the suite, the facilities are newer. No problems were found on the second night's stay. The manager also gave me a breakfast buffet for the next day.
Overall, the hotel is good and the service staff has a good attitude. After the problem was found in the parent-child suite on the first night, the room I changed to on the second night was very clean. Another problem is that when ordering takeout at the hotel, you can only put it at the front desk, and then the robot will deliver it to the room. It is safe and convenient, but there are very few robots! ! During the peak ordering period, the takeout was left at the front desk for half an hour and it couldn't be delivered! In the end, I had to go downstairs to get it myself! I hope this problem can be improved

In contrast to the efficiency of positive service, the colleagues who visited the return visit were subject to performance pressure, and the contact was very active... I will not go into details about the small problems such as the room phone not being able to dial out. Before coming this time, I heard from my father that he often received foreign guests in Gunanadu 20 years ago, and he had a good impression, so I checked out of the Central Hotel and stayed here, but what I got in return was a very different service experience. I hope the hotel will continue to work hard and contact me as soon as possible regarding the deposit issue. As a hotel practitioner, I sincerely hope that Gunanadu Group can operate this landmark hotel with care. The heavy elegance of time and the home-like service attitude should not be contradictory! Keep it up.

The front desk arranged a higher floor facing the north facing the Zifeng Building, and the scenery is not bad. The guest rooms should have been renovated without any sense of obsolescence. The room is moderate in size, warm and elegantly decorated, and I especially like the carpet pattern. The room facilities are also very complete. In order to reduce noise, the water inlet pipe of the toilet is wrapped with a thick sponge, and the downlight directly above the bathtub is specially made of frosted glass, so that the light will not be dazzling when guests lie flat in the bath. These facilities show that a hotel with a long history can gradually discover some details in the long-term operation process, and whether these details are handled properly will actually bring a very different sense of experience to the guests. It can be said that the details determine success or failure. When it comes to details, I have a bit of a hard time talking. During my stay at the hotel, I asked the floor attendant several times for something, and the waiter provided the corresponding service. However, after each service, even if it is a small service that is within the scope of the service, it is required to be named and praised on the Internet. I can understand their thoughts. This phenomenon must be related to the reward mechanism set up by the hotel, and the number of people named should also be related to income. The original intention of this mechanism is good, but the details need to be more perfect, otherwise the final effect may be counterproductive.
